if (AB_AD_TEST) {
	

	var AD_DESIGN;

	if (window['localStorage'] !== null) {

			} else {
				setTimeout(arguments.callee, 100)
			}
		}
	})();

} else {

	try{
		if (AB_AD_TEST && AD_DESIGN == 'gpt') {
			
	var gptadslots=[];
	var googletag = googletag || {};
		googletag.cmd = googletag.cmd || [];
	(function(){ var gads = document.createElement('script');
		gads.async = true; gads.type = 'text/javascript';
		var useSSL = 'https:' == document.location.protocol;
		gads.src = (useSSL ? 'https:' : 'http:') + '//www.googletagservices.com/tag/js/gpt.js';
		var node = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
		node.parentNode.insertBefore(gads, node);
	})();

	// whether or not to use the "new" or legacy ad structure
	var new_ad_structure = true;

	// default language for ad calls
	var adLanguage = 'en' != '' ? 'en' : null;

	
		
		var badgeTargets = [];
		var badgeCampaigns = [];
		
			var country = 'us' != '' ? 'us' : 'us';
			if (document.cookie) {
				var countryPattern = new RegExp("^\\s*country=\\s*(.*?)\\s*$");
				var countryCookie = document.cookie.split(";").filter(function(str) {
					return countryPattern.test(str);
				});
				if (countryCookie && countryCookie.length) country = countryCookie[0].toString().replace(countryPattern, "$1"); 
			}
			var noBadgeInCountry;	
			
				noBadgeInCountry = [];
				if (noBadgeInCountry.indexOf(country) == -1) {
					badgeTargets.push('quiz');
					
				}
			
				noBadgeInCountry = [];
				if (noBadgeInCountry.indexOf(country) == -1) {
					badgeTargets.push('bullseye');
					
				}
			

	

	function loadSwarmAds(params) {
		if (!params || !params['wid'] || !params['aclAllow']) return false;

		googletag.cmd.push(function() {
			
				gptadslots[params.wid] = defineGPTAd({ 
					wid: params.wid,
					dfp_site: 'bfd.swarm',
					platform: 'desktop',
					
					'vertical': (typeof BF_DFP_ZONE != 'Undefined' ? BF_DFP_ZONE.replace(/^\//, '') : ''),
					
					position: params.pos,
					size: params.size
				})
			
				.setTargeting('wid', params.wid)
				.setTargeting('pos', [params.pos])
				.setTargeting("nsfw", "0")	.setTargeting("user", 'minouclark').setTargeting("bid", '3945385')					;
				
				if(badgeTargets.length) {
					gptadslots[params.wid].setTargeting("badge", badgeTargets );
				}
				
				gptadslots[params.wid].addService(googletag.pubads());
			displayGPTAd({ slot: gptadslots[params.wid], wid: params.wid });
		});
	}

	function loadGPTAd(params) {
		if (!params || !params['wid']) return false;

		googletag.cmd.push(function() {

			/* New Ad Structure */
			if( params.dfp_site ) {

				// Define / Target any undefined ads
				if( !gptadslots[params.wid] ) {
					
					// Skip ridealongs for non-targeted badges
					if (
						params.targets
						&& (params.position == 'ridealong')
						&& (badgeCampaigns.indexOf(params.targets.campaign) == -1)
					) return;
					

					// Define ad
					gptadslots[params.wid] = defineGPTAd(params);
					params.slot = gptadslots[params.wid];	

					// Target ad
					if( gptadslots[params.wid] ) targetGPTAd(params);
				}

				// Display ad
				if( gptadslots[params.wid] ) displayGPTAd({ slot: gptadslots[params.wid], wid: params.wid });

				return;
			}

			/* Infinite Scroll Ad Units */
			if (params.infinite_scroll && typeof infinite_slots[params.wid] != 'undefined') {
				gptadslots[params.wid] = googletag.defineSlot('/6556/' + BF_DFP_SITE + BF_DFP_ZONE, [[5,5]],'div-gpt-ad-' + params.wid)
				.setTargeting('wid', params.wid)
				.setTargeting('pos', [infinite_slots[params.wid]])
				.setTargeting('abtest', "hptest--control_" + infinite_slots[params.wid] + "")
				.addService(googletag.pubads());
			}
			/* END Infinite Scroll Ad Units */

			/* Sidebar Ad Units */
			else if (params.sidebar) {
				var posnum = parseInt(params.wid, 10) -  4;
				gptadslots[params.wid] = googletag.defineSlot('/6556/' + BF_DFP_SITE + BF_DFP_ZONE, [[3,3]],'div-gpt-ad-' + params.wid)
				.setTargeting('wid', params.wid)
				.setTargeting('pos', ['sidebar'])
				.setTargeting('posnum', posnum).setTargeting("nsfw", "0")	.setTargeting("user", 'minouclark').setTargeting("bid", '3945385')	;
				
				if(badgeTargets.length) {
					gptadslots[params.wid].setTargeting("badge", badgeTargets );
				}
				
				gptadslots[params.wid].addService(googletag.pubads());
			}
			/* END Sidebar Ad Units */

			/* Other Site Ad Units */
			else if (typeof params['site'] != 'undefined') {
				if (!params['size']) return false;
				gptadslots[params.wid] = googletag.defineSlot('/6556/bfd.widget/' + params.site, [params.size],'div-gpt-ad-' + params.wid)
					.setTargeting('wid', params.wid)
					.setTargeting('site', params.site)
					.addService(googletag.pubads());
			}
			/* END Other Site Ad Units */

			/* Weekend Promo Ad Unit */
			if (params.sitewideweekend) {
				gptadslots[params.wid] = googletag.defineSlot('/6556/' + BF_DFP_SITE + BF_DFP_ZONE, [[5,5]],'div-gpt-ad-' + params.wid)
					.setTargeting('wid', params.wid)
					.setTargeting('pos',['sitewideweekend']).setTargeting("nsfw", "0")	.setTargeting("user", 'minouclark').setTargeting("bid", '3945385')	;
				
				if(badgeTargets.length) {
					gptadslots[params.wid].setTargeting("badge", badgeTargets );
				}
				
				gptadslots[params.wid].addService(googletag.pubads());
			}
			/* END Weekend Promo Ad Unit */

			/* Ridealong Ad Unit */
			else if (params.campaign && !gptadslots[params.wid]) {
				
				if(badgeCampaigns.indexOf(params.campaign) == -1) {
					return;
				}
				
				gptadslots[params.wid] = googletag.defineSlot('/6556/bfd.badge' , [params.size],'div-gpt-ad-' + params.wid)
					.setTargeting('wid', params.wid)
					.setTargeting('pos', [params.pos])
					.setTargeting('campaign', params.campaign).setTargeting("nsfw", "0")	.setTargeting("user", 'minouclark').setTargeting("bid", '3945385')	;
				
				if(badgeTargets.length) {
					gptadslots[params.wid].setTargeting("badge", badgeTargets );
				}
				
				gptadslots[params.wid].addService(googletag.pubads());
			}
			/* END Ridealong Ad Unit */

			else if (params.pos && !gptadslots[params.wid]) {
				gptadslots[params.wid] = googletag.defineSlot('/6556/' + BF_DFP_SITE + BF_DFP_ZONE, [params.size],'div-gpt-ad-' + params.wid)
				
					.setTargeting('wid', params.wid)
					.setTargeting('pos', [params.pos])
					
					.setTargeting("nsfw", "0")	.setTargeting("user", 'minouclark').setTargeting("bid", '3945385')	;
						
						if(badgeTargets.length) {
							gptadslots[params.wid].setTargeting("badge", badgeTargets );
						}
						
						gptadslots[params.wid]
					
				
				.addService(googletag.pubads());
			}
			displayGPTAd({ slot: gptadslots[params.wid], wid: params.wid });
		});
	}

	function loadGPTCompanions() {
	    window.BF_DFP_MSU = true;
	    loadGPTAd({ 'wid': 26, 'pos': 'msu', 'size': [100, 100] });
	}

	function defineGPTAd(params) {
		if(!params) return;

		// Optional parameters
		var vertical = params.vertical;
		var position = params.position;
		var language = params.language || adLanguage;
		var foreign_country = false;
		if(typeof BF_STATIC != 'undefined') {
			foreign_country = BF_STATIC.country != 'us';
			if(!language) {
				if( BF_STATIC.country == 'mx' ) {
					language = 'mx';
				}else if( BF_STATIC.country == 'es-es' ) {		
					language = 'sp';		
				}else{		
					language = ( BF_STATIC.language != '' ) ? BF_STATIC.language : 'en';
				}		
			}
		}
		var test_env = '';
		if(window.location.search.match("adtest") !== null) {
			test_env = '.test';
		} else if (window.location.search.match("giraffe_test") !== null) {
			test_env = '.giraffe_test';
		} else if (window.location.search.match("adops_giraffe") !== null) {
			test_env = '.adops_giraffe';
		}

		// Required parameters
		var wid = params.wid;
		var legacy_structure = params.legacy_structure;
		var dfp_site = params.dfp_site;
		var platform = params.platform;
		var size = params.size;
		if(!wid || !( ( dfp_site && platform && language) || legacy_structure ) || !size) {
			console.error("Error: defineGPTAd requires additional parameters");
			return;
		}

		if(!vertical || vertical == '') { 
						// Add missing vertical info for plugins
			vertical = 'culture';

			// Set vertical to value in div.page[data-role="page"][data-uri]
			if(vertical == '') {
				var page = document.getElementsByClassName('page');
				for (i = 0; i < page.length; i++) {
					var div = page[i];
					if(div.getAttribute('data-role') == 'page') {
						vertical = div.getAttribute('data-uri');
						break;
					}
				}
			}

			// Set vertical to BF_DFP_ZONE
			if((typeof BF_DFP_ZONE != 'undefined') && (vertical == '')) vertical = BF_DFP_ZONE.replace(/\//, '');

			// Set vertical to other by default
			if(vertical == '') vertical = 'other';
		}

		// Set vertical index to home
		if(vertical.match(/^index(beta)?$/)) vertical = 'home';
		if(vertical && (foreign_country || vertical == 'usnews')) {
			// Set uknews, aunews, usnews, francenews, etc to 'news'
			vertical = vertical.replace(/.*news$/, 'news');
			// Set francebuzz, ukbuzz, etc to 'buzz'
			vertical = vertical.replace(/.*buzz$/, 'buzz');
		}

		var slotURL;
		if( legacy_structure ) {
			slotURL = '/6556/' + ( position == 'ridealong' ? 'bfd.badge' : BF_DFP_SITE + BF_DFP_ZONE );
		} else {
			slotURL = '/6556/' + dfp_site + test_env + '.' + platform + '/' + language + '/' + vertical + (position ? '/' + position : '');
		}
		var slot = googletag.defineSlot(slotURL, [params.size],'div-gpt-ad-' + wid);

		if (vertical.match(/videos/i)) {
			if (document.cookie && +wid === 13) {
				var abPattern = new RegExp("^\\s*abeagle_videos_test=\\s*(.*?)\\s*$");
				var abCookie = document.cookie.split(";").filter(function(str) {
					return abPattern.test(str);
				})[0].split('=')[1];
				if (abCookie.match(/control/i)) {
					slot.setTargeting('abtest', 'controlvideos_bigstory');
				}
			}
		}

		return slot;
	}

	function targetGPTAd(params) {
        // Slot and targets objects are required
		if(!params || !params.slot || !params.targets) {
			console.error("Error: targetGPTAd requires additional parameters");
			return;
		}

		// Required parameters
		var slot = params.slot;
		var targets = params.targets;

		// Optional parameters
		var user = params.user;
		var target_buzz = params.target_buzz;

		// Add missing targeting info for plugins
		if(target_buzz && !user) {
			
				targets.nsfw = '0';
				targets.user = 'minouclark';
				
				targets.bid = '3945385';
				
				
				if(badgeTargets.length) {
					targets.badge = badgeTargets;
				}
				
			
		}

		
		// Ensure the correct badges are being targeted 
		if(params.targets && params.targets.badge) {
			if (badgeTargets.length) {
				params.targets.badge = badgeTargets;
			}else {
				delete params.targets.badge;
			}
		}
		

		// Set targeted values 	
		for (var key in targets) {
			if(targets[key]) slot.setTargeting(key, targets[key]);
		}
		slot.addService(googletag.pubads());
		return slot;
	}

	function displayGPTAd(params) {
		// Slot and wid args are required
		if(!params || !params.slot || !params.wid) {
			console.error("Error: displayGPTAd requires additional parameters");
			return;
		}

		
		// Display msu companion ad
		if ((params.wid == 13) && gptadslots[26] && document.getElementById('div-gpt-ad-26')){
			displayGPTAd({ slot: gptadslots[26], wid: 26 });
		}
		

		// Log to sessionStorage for selenium testing
		if (window.location.search.substring(1).match(/selenium\=true/g) && window.sessionStorage) {
			logGPTAd(params.slot);	
		}
		// Display ad if we're not testing
		else {
			googletag.display('div-gpt-ad-' + params.wid);
			
		}

		return params.slot;
	}

	function logGPTAd(slot) {
		// Slot and wid args are required
		if(!slot) {
			console.error("Error: logGPTAd requires additional parameters");
			return;
		}

		// Get targeted values 
		var targets = {};
		var target_keys = slot.getTargetingKeys();
		for (var i = 0; i < target_keys.length; i++) {
			var key = target_keys[i];
			targets[key] = slot.getTargeting(key).toString();
		}

		// update the total ad count for this page
		if(targets.wid) {
			if(!sessionStorage.getItem('gpt_ad_'+targets.wid)) {
				var ad_count = sessionStorage.getItem('gpt_ad_count');
				ad_count = ad_count ? parseInt(ad_count) : 0;
				sessionStorage.setItem('gpt_ad_count', ad_count+1 );
			}
			// never save abtest info, which frequently changes
			delete targets.abtest;
			// list targets in alphabetical order 
			var ttargets = {};
			var keys = Object.keys(targets).sort();
			keys.forEach(function(value, index) {
				if(value in targets) ttargets[value] = targets[value];
			});
			targets = ttargets;
			// add url and size to log
			var sizes = slot.getSizes();
			var size = [];
			if(sizes.length) {
				sizes = sizes[0]; 
				for (k in sizes) {
					if(typeof sizes[k] == 'number') size.push(sizes[k]);
				}
			}
			var gpt_ad = {
				'targets': targets,
				'url': slot.getAdUnitPath(),
				'size': size.length ? size.join('x') : '',
			};
			// store the parameters passed to loadGPTAd
			sessionStorage.setItem('gpt_ad_'+targets.wid, JSON.stringify(gpt_ad));

		}
		return slot;
	}

	googletag.cmd.push(function() {
		
		// expected ads for SRA
		var expected_ads = [{"wid":13,"targets":{"wid":13,"bid":"3945385","badge":["quiz","bullseye"],"user":"minouclark","pos":"bigstory-bp","nsfw":"0"},"language":"en","position":"bigstory-bp","target_buzz":1,"size":[5,5],"vertical":"culture","dfp_site":"bfd","platform":"desktop"},{"targets":{"wid":26,"bid":"3945385","badge":["quiz","bullseye"],"user":"minouclark","pos":"bigstory-bp","nsfw":"0"},"wid":26,"language":"en","position":"bigstory-bp","target_buzz":1,"size":[100,100],"vertical":"culture","platform":"desktop","dfp_site":"bfd"},{"wid":9,"targets":{"wid":9,"bid":"3945385","badge":["quiz","bullseye"],"user":"minouclark","pos":"story-bpage","nsfw":"0"},"language":"en","position":"story-bpage","target_buzz":1,"size":[5,5],"vertical":"culture","dfp_site":"bfd","platform":"desktop"},{}];

		if (expected_ads.length) {
			// Pre-define and target each of the expected_ads
			expected_ads.forEach(function(ad) {
                if (!ad.wid) return;

				
				// Skip ridealongs for non-targeted badges
				if (
					ad.targets
					&& (ad.position == 'ridealong')
					&& (badgeCampaigns.indexOf(ad.targets.campaign) == -1)
				) return;
				

				// Set up ad 
				if (!gptadslots[ad.wid]) {
					// Define ad
					gptadslots[ad.wid] = defineGPTAd(ad);
					ad.slot = gptadslots[ad.wid];
					// Target ad
					if (gptadslots[ad.wid]) targetGPTAd(ad);
				}
			});
		}
		
		googletag.pubads().setTargeting('poe', BF_REFERER);
		googletag.pubads().setTargeting('abtest', AD_DESIGN);
		googletag.pubads().setTargeting('ord', BF_DFP_ORD.toString());
		/* Add DFP Tag Terms */
		googletag.pubads().setTargeting('tag', [''] );
		
		googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {
			var slot = event.slot;

			// Get targeted values 
			var targets = {};
			var target_keys = slot.getTargetingKeys();
			for (var i = 0; i < target_keys.length; i++) {
				var key = target_keys[i];
				targets[key] = slot.getTargeting(key).toString();
			}	
		
			// Determine whether ad loaded successfully
			var loaded = !event.isEmpty && event.size && event.size[0] && event.size[1];

			// Return from slotRenderEnded if nothing is targeted
			if(!targets) return;

			// Pinterest ads
			if(targets.pos && targets.pos.match('pinterest')) {
				if(loaded && document.getElementsByClassName('hot-on-pinterest').length) {	
					var pinterestunit = document.getElementsByClassName('hot-on-pinterest')[0];
					if(bf_pinterest_referer) {
						// Vertical pages
						if(bf_pinterest_referer.PAGE_TYPE == 'vertical') {
							// Move pinterestunit to prominent position in sidebar
							if(document.getElementsByClassName('Column2').length) {
								var sidebar = document.getElementsByClassName('Column2')[0];
								if(sidebar.firstChild != pinterestunit) sidebar.insertBefore(pinterestunit, sidebar.firstChild);
							}
						// Bpages
						}else if(bf_pinterest_referer.PAGE_TYPE == 'bpage') {
							pinterestunit.style.cssText = 'margin-top: 30px !important';
							// Unhide sponsored pinterest unit on bpage
							pinterestunit.className = pinterestunit.className.replace(/\s+hidden/g, '');
						}else if(bf_pinterest_referer.PAGE_TYPE == 'bpage-mobile') {
							// Unhide sponsored pinterest unit on bpage
							pinterestunit.className = pinterestunit.className.replace(/\s+hidden/g, '');
						}
					}
					// hide backfill buzz
					if(targets.wid == '33') {
						var backfill = document.getElementsByClassName("pinterest-list__li js-backfill");
						if(backfill.length) backfill[0].className += ' hidden';	
					}
					// show ad unit
					var ad_unit = document.getElementById('BF_WIDGET_'+targets.wid).parentNode;
					ad_unit.className = ad_unit.className.replace(/\s+hidden/g, '');
				}
			// Headerstrip ads
			} else if(targets.wid && (targets.wid == '10')) {
				if(loaded) {
					// remove backfill buzz
					var backfill = document.getElementsByClassName("unit js-backfill");
					if(backfill.length) backfill[0].remove();
					// show ad unit
					var ad_unit = document.getElementById('div-gpt-ad-'+targets.wid).parentNode.parentNode;
					ad_unit.className = ad_unit.className.replace(/\s+hidden/g, '');
				}
			// Top SWARM ads
			} else if(targets.wid && (targets.wid == '41' || targets.wid == '40')) {
				if (loaded) {
					// show ad unit
					var ad_unit = document.getElementById('BF_WIDGET_'+targets.wid);
					ad_unit.className = ad_unit.className.replace(/\s+hidden/g, '');
				}
			}

		});
		googletag.pubads().enableAsyncRendering();		googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();		googletag.enableServices();
	});

		}
	} catch(err) { console.log(err); }

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
  (function () {
    if (BF_STATIC.os === 'ios' && BF_STATIC.app_name === 'bfnews' && BF_STATIC.app_version >= 10050000) {
      document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
        var user_url = 'bf://author/view?feed_url=';
        $('.user-bylines div.byline, .user-bylines div.user-info').each(function(){
          var anchors = $(this).find('span, a.byline, a.byline__author');
          var href = $(anchors[0]).attr('href');
          var username = href.match(/\/([^\/]*)$/)[1];
          var base_url = encodeURIComponent(window.location.origin + BF_STATIC.web_root + '/api/v1/feeds/' + username);
          anchors.each(function(){
            if (!$(this).attr('href')) return
            var a = $('<a>' + $(this).html() + '</a>');;
            var attributes = this.attributes;
            $.each(attributes, function (index) {
              if (attributes[index].name == 'href') {
                $(a).attr('href', user_url + base_url);
              } else {
                $(a).attr(attributes[index].name, attributes[index].value);
              }
            });
            $(this).after(a).remove();
          });
        });
      });
    }
  })();
</script>

<div class="quiz_tally_results bf_dom" rel:ab_test="quiz_results_percentile" rel:bf_bucket="abtest" rel:tweet_via="buzzfeeders" style="display: none;">
<h2>Can We Guess Your Personality Based On Your Taste In Cheese?</h2>
<div class="headline-1 quiz_tally"></div>
<div class="js-quiz-percentile quiz__percentile-title"></div>
<ol>
<li class="quiz_result has_result_image" data-id="7767402" rel:description="You’re a free spirit, always open to new experiences and down to go with the flow. Whether you’re trying foreign cheeses or meeting new people, you always find a way to enjoy every adventure life throws your way." rel:id="7767402" rel:name="Creative &amp; open-minded" rel:range_end="0" rel:range_start="0" style="display:none">
<h2 class="headline-1">
								
									You got:
								
								Creative &amp; open-minded
							</h2>
<p>You’re a free spirit, always open to new experiences and down to go with the flow. Whether you’re trying foreign cheeses or meeting new people, you always find a way to enjoy every adventure life throws your way.</p>
<div class="headline-1 answer_response"></div>
<div class="quiz_img_and_source">
<img class="result_img" data:src="https://img.buzzfeed.com/buzzfeed-static/static/2015-08/11/11/enhanced/webdr05/anigif_enhanced-30754-1439305382-11.gif" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAPAAAAAAAAAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw=="/>
<span class="sub_buzz_source_via buzz_attribution">NBC / Via <a href="http://giphy.com/gifs/jennifer-lawrence-wink-sassy-WS0PntIm3nExG" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">giphy.com</a></span>
</div>
</li>
<li class="quiz_result has_result_image" data-id="7767403" rel:description="You’re cultured and well-traveled. Whether you’re challenging your palette with new cheesy flavors or hopping on a plane to a faraway land, you’re always down for an exciting new experience. You’re all about spontaneity and living in the moment." rel:id="7767403" rel:name="Adventurous &amp; worldly" rel:range_end="0" rel:range_start="0" style="display:none">
<h2 class="headline-1">
								
									You got:
								
								Adventurous &amp; worldly
							</h2>
<p>You’re cultured and well-traveled. Whether you’re challenging your palette with new cheesy flavors or hopping on a plane to a faraway land, you’re always down for an exciting new experience. You’re all about spontaneity and living in the moment.</p>
<div class="headline-1 answer_response"></div>
<div class="quiz_img_and_source">
<img class="result_img" data:src="https://img.buzzfeed.com/buzzfeed-static/static/2015-08/11/11/enhanced/webdr01/anigif_enhanced-9320-1439305350-3.gif" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAPAAAAAAAAAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw=="/>
<span class="sub_buzz_source_via buzz_attribution">Big Machine Records / Via <a href="http://giphy.com/gifs/taylor-swift-bad-blood-VMfSovESs0BJ6" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">giphy.com</a></span>
</div>
</li>
<li class="quiz_result has_result_image" data-id="7767404" rel:description="You’re incredibly suave and enjoy the finer things life has to offer. It’s clear from your refined taste in cheese that you’re never one to settle for any less than you deserve. You see nothing wrong with high standards and going after what you want." rel:id="7767404" rel:name="Classy &amp; debonair" rel:range_end="0" rel:range_start="0" style="display:none">
<h2 class="headline-1">
								
									You got:
								
								Classy &amp; debonair
							</h2>
<p>You’re incredibly suave and enjoy the finer things life has to offer. It’s clear from your refined taste in cheese that you’re never one to settle for any less than you deserve. You see nothing wrong with high standards and going after what you want.</p>
<div class="headline-1 answer_response"></div>
<div class="quiz_img_and_source">
<img class="result_img" data:src="https://img.buzzfeed.com/buzzfeed-static/static/2015-08/11/11/enhanced/webdr06/anigif_enhanced-29873-1439305330-7.gif" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAPAAAAAAAAAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw=="/>

</div>
</li>
<li class="quiz_result has_result_image" data-id="7767405" rel:description="You have a great sense of humor and always know how to make those around you smile. Your enthusiasm is infectious and your zest for life is inspirational. You know better than to judge a cheese by its cover and same goes for your fun-loving approach to life." rel:id="7767405" rel:name="Funny &amp; spontaneous" rel:range_end="0" rel:range_start="0" style="display:none">
<h2 class="headline-1">
								
									You got:
								
								Funny &amp; spontaneous
							</h2>
<p>You have a great sense of humor and always know how to make those around you smile. Your enthusiasm is infectious and your zest for life is inspirational. You know better than to judge a cheese by its cover and same goes for your fun-loving approach to life.</p>
<div class="headline-1 answer_response"></div>
<div class="quiz_img_and_source">
<img class="result_img" data:src="https://img.buzzfeed.com/buzzfeed-static/static/2015-08/11/11/enhanced/webdr06/anigif_enhanced-30490-1439305278-2.gif" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAPAAAAAAAAAAACH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAICRAEAOw=="/>
<span class="sub_buzz_source_via buzz_attribution">Comedy Central / Via <a href="http://giphy.com/gifs/amy-schumer-inside-amber-tamblyn-EOlcvQfnnSMM0" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">giphy.com</a></span>
</div>
</li>
<li class="quiz_result has_result_image" data-id="7767406" rel:description="You’re outspoken, sarcastic, opinionated, and not afraid to show it. To you there’s no point wasting time with formalities, you like to skip right to the chase and get to the heart of the matter. Your strong opinions of cheese are also reflected in how you handle most life experiences. There’s no time for BS with you, honey!" rel:id="7767406" rel:name="Spunky &amp; sassy" rel:range_end="0" rel:range_start="0" style="display:none">
<h2 class="headline-1">
								
									You got:
								
								Spunky &amp; sassy
							</h2>
<p>You’re outspoken, sarcastic, opinionated, and not afraid to show it. To you there’s no point wasting time with formalities, you like to skip right to the chase and get to the heart of the matter. Your strong opinions of cheese are also reflected in how you handle most life experiences. There’s no time for BS with you, honey!</p>
<div class="headline-1 answer_response"></div>

<span class="sub_buzz_source_via buzz_attribution">Paramount Pictures / Via <a href="http://giphy.com/gifs/clueless-as-if-guys-hshZwZemt0r28" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">giphy.com</a></span>
</div>
</li>
<li class="quiz_result has_result_image" data-id="7767407" rel:description="You’re sensitive and in touch with your emotional side. One of your best qualities is that you’re incredibly caring and considerate toward others. People know you as a reliable and genuine person who can always be counted on. The world needs more wonderful people like you!" rel:id="7767407" rel:name="Thoughtful &amp; loving" rel:range_end="0" rel:range_start="0" style="display:none">
<h2 class="headline-1">
								
									You got:
								
								Thoughtful &amp; loving
							</h2>
<p>You’re sensitive and in touch with your emotional side. One of your best qualities is that you’re incredibly caring and considerate toward others. People know you as a reliable and genuine person who can always be counted on. The world needs more wonderful people like you!</p>

<script type="text/javascript">
function loadScript(script) {
    var deferred = Q.defer();
    var scriptEl = document.createElement('script');
    scriptEl.setAttribute('type', 'text/javascript');
    scriptEl.setAttribute('src', script);
    scriptEl.onload = function() {
        deferred.resolve();
    };
    document.body.appendChild(scriptEl);
    return deferred.promise;
}

EventManager.observe_once(
    "acl:load:done",
    function() {
        var u = new BF_User();
        if (u) {
            u = u.getUserInfo();
        }
        if (acl.user_can('duplicate_post') || acl.user_can('feedback_tool')) {
            var scriptEl = document.createElement('script');
            scriptEl.setAttribute('type', 'text/javascript');
            scriptEl.setAttribute('src', 'https://webappstatic.buzzfeed.com/static/js/public/q/q.js');
        }

        scriptEl.onload = function() {

            if (acl.user_can('feedback_tool')) {
                Q.all([
                  loadScript('https://webappstatic.buzzfeed.com/static/js/html2canvas/html2canvas.js'),
                  loadScript('https://webappstatic.buzzfeed.com/static/js/t3/services/user.js?v=1471018737'),
                  loadScript('https://webappstatic.buzzfeed.com/static/js/t3/services/image-proxier.js?v=1471018737'),
                  loadScript('https://webappstatic.buzzfeed.com/static/js/t3/modules/feedback-widget-trigger.js?v=1471018737'),
                  loadScript('https://webappstatic.buzzfeed.com/static/js/t3/modules/feedback-widget.js?v=1471018737'),
                  loadScript('https://webappstatic.buzzfeed.com/static/js/t3/modules/screenshot-canvas.js?v=1471018737'),
                ])
                .then(function() {
                  var triggerEl = document.querySelector('.js-usernav-feedback');
                  triggerEl.setAttribute('data-module', 'feedback-widget-trigger');
                  Box.Application.start(triggerEl); // like init but for a single module

                  var widgetEl = document.querySelector('.js-feedback-widget');
                  widgetEl.setAttribute('data-module', 'feedback-widget');
                  Box.Application.start(widgetEl); // like init but for a single module

                  var canvasEl = document.querySelector('.js-screenshot-canvas');
                  canvasEl.setAttribute('data-module', 'screenshot-canvas');
                  Box.Application.start(canvasEl);
                });
            }
            if (acl.user_can('duplicate_post')) {
              Q.all([
                  loadScript('https://webappstatic.buzzfeed.com/static/js/t3/modules/superduper.js?v=1471018737')
                ])
                .then(function() {
                  var triggerEl = document.querySelector('[data-module="superduper"]');
                  Box.Application.start(triggerEl); // like init but for a single module
                });

            }
            
        }
        document.body.appendChild(scriptEl);
    }
);

</script>
